< Review>
So, I'm pretty sure the "Quickly" for its name can be applied to the drinks they make, but definitely not for the food. i went there for an hour lunch break; big mistake! It took 30 minutes for the food I ordered (a fairly simple noodle bowl) to be be made. Even then, the food was poorly made. The chicken was slimy and the soup broth was really generic. Not very flavorful.

After eating what I could to make it back to work on time, I started feeling sick an hour later. My stomach clearly didn't like the food.

Go there for your drinks, sure, but definitely not for the food!</Review>

</record></dataset><record>
< text>
The wait here can be ridiculous. If you're standing in line behind 4 people, you can expect at least two people to order an Oreo shake, which takes the cashier a few minutes to prep. I've waited upwards of 20 minutes to get my order in on a basic Jasmine Milk Tea.

This is a decent place for a no-frills, cheap milk tea. If the line is too long or you're willing to spend a little more, try Boba Loca on the other side of the plaza, or Sharetea in Todos Los Santos. Chances are driving there will be faster than waiting in line here for your order.</text>

Take the winding roads of Topanga Canyon to get up to the trailhead. It‚Äôs a short walk to a fork in the road. If you turn left, you‚Äôll head up 0.4 miles to a point where you can see the Santa Monica Pier. There‚Äôs one bench and a stone ‚Äúlabyrinth‚Äù which is fun to circle around in. If you take a right and keep following the road right, there‚Äôs a ~1.7 mile trail that leads to an end where there‚Äôs a smaller stone ‚Äúlabyrinth‚Äù and a view of the Malibu Pier. If you want to add onto the hike, you could also veer towards the water tank, which is a separate trail.

Parking is free but be sure to park on the pavement. You‚Äôll definitely need your parallel parking skills to be on point, or just just keep going down the road to find a spot. There‚Äôs no bathrooms or water fountains so bring plenty of water! The trail is very exposed with minimal shade from the trees. There‚Äôs a slight gradient uphill when you turn left, and it‚Äôs a slight gradient downhill when you turn right. Overall it‚Äôs a fun, free way to get some steps in. Enjoy the fresh air and ocean breeze!< /Text>< Pictures>

< Review>
Tuna Canyon Trailhead is a beautiful hiking trail located between the mountain ranges between Malibu and Topanga. The entrance is slightly hidden, but the trail itself offers some stunning views from the city of LA to the valleys and beaches of Malibu. The trail is quite wide and is really more of a hilly walk than a rigorous hike. Overall, I had a wonderful experience here, and hope to come back soon for some of the most romantic viewpoints in the greater Los Angeles area!< /Review>

<Rating>5< /Rating><text>As a hiker I don‚Äôt say this lightly that the Tuna Canyon Trail has the most spectacular and stunning view. TC Park has 1,255-acre in the western Santa Monica Mountains above PCH in Malibu parallels more than two miles of the Pacific Ocean, and provides dramatic, 360-degree views of the San Gabriel mountains to the Santa Monica Bay. Furthermore, it links over 18,000 acres of contiguous protected open space from Topanga State Park west to Las Flores Canyon. We drove up to the trail head from PCH via narrow Tuna Canyon road. There‚Äôs only dirt parking near and/or at the trail head. The entrance to the trail is somewhat hidden and the only landmark is that huge rusty white painted guard metal gate entrance. The hike is about 2 to 5.1 miles (out and back) with elevation change of 900 to 1,500 ft. The trail head has two main
view points: the West vp (Hearst Tank) and the East vp (Big Rock Lateral). Both view points are not interconnected albeit offer a magnificent 360 degrees view of the park. The park is located in Topanga Canyon and it‚Äôs dog and bike friendly. The trails were flat and wide with few rocky sections. It took us approximately 2 hrs and 45 minutes to complete both trail sections. We like that this trails are not as crowded and no human traffic. We were breathless when there were literally an ocean of clouds like cotton candy blanketing the pacific ocean, Santa Monica Bay and Malibu. Overall, I highly recommend this trail. A perfect hiking spot for beginners or experienced hiker.</text><pics>None</pics><response>None<//response><gmapID>0x80c2a1aedb74078f:0x8f883fb02c31c746<//gmapID></record></dataset><record>

I have bought cards from Channel Fireball a few times. Shipping is a bit expensive to my country but the experience was pretty good.
I bought cards for one of my friends as well, CB couldn't find all the cards we ordered. They gave us an options to resolve it, cashback, alternative card quality, my friend wasn't disappointment and I got my money back from him.
They never sent me scratched cards as near mint. Highly recommend.
They have free podcasts for magic the gathering as well called limited resources. Thanks guys!< /review>

<rating>4</rating>< review>
The place is designed with being able to play card games in mind. Theres a toooon of tables. More than I've ever seen at any non tour atmosphere and it's amazing. They have snacks, packs, singles, matts etc. They have a bit of everything you will need. Only reason it's not a 5 star is they only support standard in store. The single they have are for standard, the format, packs etc are all for standard. They of course have lands, Nicol bolas and a few other high end non standard cards. But they have the real estate to support more than just standard.</review>

<UserId.>107968783541319464850< /UserId.><name>Michael Xing</name>< time>
1391746866080< /time>
<rating>5</rating>< Text>
From a purely aesthetic standpoint, the game center isn't much. It's a warehouse-y space located in a odd corner near the San Jose Airport; the decor and amenities are worn but well-kept. What really makes this place shine is the great staff and the community. Especially if you're a Magic: The Gathering fan this is place to be for events, trading, and collecting. Tons of players flock here for Friday drafts, release events, and just to hang out. The staff is super friendly and they have great MTG judge support. Sometimes a taco stand will show up (appropriately named "Tapped Out Tacos") to provide burritos and soda. Couldn't really ask for much more from a game store.< /Text>

We dropped in Smitty's for some to-go benefits on our means to Hess. We had actually both avoided lunch that day, so we were starving when the great girl at the register asked us what appeared excellent.\"Everything!\" wasn't the ideal response, though it was the fact. She did inform us that the sections were large, yet provided our famished state, we downplayed it.I purchased the combination plate (chicken and ribs, with sides of macaroni as well as collard greens) and also my partner opted for the Friday night unique, the deep-fried catfish, which was served with fries. < review>

"GET OVER HERE! "
If it weren't for my quick wit and narrow escape that followed by a shrug to my girlfriend and turning around I sincerely doubt that I would be with enough life in me to write this review now.

<Rating>1< /Rating><user_id>108554251298922423991</user_id><name>Michael Frasco< /name>< Text>
I bought a new house in a nice neighborhood and wanted to have a good pest control service to keep the bugs at bay.  Jake was going door to door and did a house evaluation.  He was able to point out areas of concern and even found a number of black widows with egg sacks.  The initial price was $129 per quarter for complete treatment with unlimited retreats for free. We went over all my areas of concern with fleas, flies, mosquitoes, silver fish and gnats.  The first service was good, the tech seemed to know what he was doing and was professional. My only complaint was that the tech was not able to fully treat my Ivy wall as I specifically asked Jake about.  He said that the sales guys are from Utah and dont know California regulations.  Apparently they arent allowed to treat anything over 4 feet.  SO if i have an 8' tall green wall that is bug and spider central, they cant treat it.   Over the course of the month after the treatment I noticed a significant increase in bug activity.  I called.  It took 4 calls and then be put on a call back list to talk to someone.   The service tech came, at an unannounced time, far after the scheduled appointment.  He then said that my watering was the problem. Now I am not a bug specialist, but I water 5 minutes at a shot 4 days/week.  That doesn't seem like a lot.  I also have it set to manual mode, so the sprinklers are not going off without my knowledge.  I am not over watering.  Then to my suprise, he hands me another $129 bill.  he said because its the start of a new quarter, there is another charge.  My first treatment was in June. < review>
DO NOT FALL FOR THIS. They have very persuasive and pushy sales people that will stop at nothing to get you to sign the contract and pay right away. They will result to guilt tactics and seemingly give you "special and exclusive discounts" if you sign up right away. They know people are going to push back so they've hiked their prices up in order to "discount" them in front of you to hook you into signing a very long and deceptive contract.

*If you've already signed the contract, then YOU HAVE 3 BUSINESS DAYS TO CANCEL WITHOUT PENALTY otherwise you'll be charged a hefty $249-$349 cancellation fee. Make sure to sign and date Page 3 of the contract (the page that says "Notice of Cancellation" at the top) and email it or drop it off in person within 3 business days of signing the contract.

By the way, the sales person did not mention the contract cancellation fee until I kept digging and asking more questions. Finally they said they'd knock it down from $349 to $200. After the sales person left, I read the contract and it had $249 listed as a cancellation fee. Super DECEPTIVE. *Read the contract before you sign anything.*

Also, they should not be sending Sales people DOOR to DOOR during the CORONAVIRUS pandemic. It is NOT over yet. There are spikes in cases every day and most of the houses in my neighborhood they are pitching to are elderly and at risk. This is horrible business practice. Also the sales person was not wearing a mask.

This review is NOT a review on their actual service. I cannot attest to whether or not it is quality or worth the price. However, even if the services were good, there are plenty of other decent pest control companies with honest and upfront business practices and pricing.
